The evidence base, collected by investigators of the Security Service of Ukraine, allowed the responsibility of another enemy associate, which was transferred by the occupiers of the dislocation of the Defense Forces in Mykolaiv region.

First of all, he tried to install and send the aggressor locations of armor and other fortifications of the Armed Forces near the regional center.

SBU staff detained the attacker at the end of June 2022 during the contradictory measures in the frontal territories of the region.

According to the materials of the Ukrainian special service, the court appointed him 8 years in prison, taking into account his cooperation with the investigation.

According to the investigation, the attacker is a local resident who, at the beginning of the full -scale invasion of the Russian Federation, was remotely involved by the FSB in the unlawful work.

It is established that the Russian intelligence service went to a man through one Ordrekmlivsky telegrams, where he has repeatedly left his anti-Ukrainian comments.

He carried out all further communication with the FSB in the messenger through the "liaison". He was the administrator of the same telegram channel.

The invaders planned to use the positions of Ukrainian defenders to prepare rocket and artillery shelling.

On the basis of the evidence collected, the court found a hostile informant guilty of the two -way of the Criminal Code of Ukraine:

▪️ Part 3 of Art. 114-2(Unauthorized dissemination of information about the direction, movement of weapons, weapons and ammunition to Ukraine, movement, displacement of the Armed Forces or other military formations formed in accordance with the laws of Ukraine);

▪ 1. 2 you. 3 st. 436-2(justification, recognition legitimate, denial of armed aggression of the Russian Federation against Ukraine, glorification of its participants).

Front guns are testing a unique complex- "Invisible" arthraun: Report from "zeros"

Author: ['Віктор Шевченко']

Time: 2023-06-27T81:00:00-04:00

Description: Ukrainian Army Daedalus BISH WID WIDELIKH RADYANSKY METHODIV Delivery, ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest News today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when, the war with Ukraine in 2022 Whether there will be a year or not, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukraine’s news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['golovna-50.jpg', '1-88.jpg', 'bez-ymeny-koe1.jpg', 'foto-3-19.jpg', 'jtjt-150x150.jpg', '5-55-150x150.jpg', '6-50.jpg']

Tags: ['ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ГАРМАШІ']

Category: News

_ The Ukrainian army is increasingly moving away from outdated Soviet management methods, mastering the latest domestic developments. Remember, for example, the introduction of a protected combat system of management of the tactical link "Nettle", without which no combat unit now does? Now the Armed Forces have every chance of weaponing another unique development _ — an automated and remote control system of artillery intelligence barak, which cannot be detected by any technical means. And this is because it gives a clear "tight" of the coordinates of the work of even a large caliber -gun at a distance of 12 km, and mortars and artillery — ** _ up to 30 km.

Correspondent ArmyinformHe had a conversation about this development with the chief of artillery of one of the individual infantry brigades that nowadays the invaders in the Donetsk direction. Lieutenant Colonel Vitaliy Podvysotsky Testatta helps to improve the truly unique invention of his author and his large team of like -minded people for almost a year. According to him, the development is already practical to wide use in the Armed Forces.

*!

  • This development appeared in us last summer, after the beginning of the Great War. In her minds, we needed to have the most effective means of counteracting the occupiers, based on the correlation of our forces and means. What we did not meet us for many reasons, including the moral and physical obsolescence of the Soviet model systems. It is a very painful topic for artillery. Therefore, when we met the Odessa inventor scientist, who was already related to the development of acoustic intelligence systems, we have started active cooperation.

Honestly, I did not believe at first that barak would work effectively when a team of like -minded people and colleagues of the inventor with some thamphon and microphones came to the front. But we urgently needed some new tool of artillery intelligence, first of all, for an effective counter -battery fight against the enemy. Therefore, we joined their work, and in the summer of Odessa we were given to us for testing a pilot version of the complex barak.

  • What bar k is self -and physically?

The first version of the barracks

But at the moment we have reached the next. Now we are filled with accurate coordinating articles and individual enemy guns at distances of up to 30 kilometers. We have the most accurate data if we fire from distances of U18-24 kilometers. We spend no more than five seconds on "sampling". After that, with the help of barak operators, we compare our data with the data of our "birds", which are almost constantly spreading in the sky and are with operators_Barak_ on direct communication online, information from tactical intelligence, we get the same coordinates of goals.

  • Mr. Vitaliy, what is this complex physically?

  • It is easy to work, does not require large human or material costs. Physically, it is eight, and, if necessary, small, small modules of directional action, which are located according to certain schemes of tacked, for several kilometers. They work around the clock, independently of each other, having every energy supply for 5-7 days. Software is constantly being improved taking into account various factors that fall to the work of the complex. It is the intensity and massness of the work of the gate -artillery, each barrel of which barak should be astonished, the time of day, the temperature environment, etc. The latest updates that have made for barak Odessa are an opportunity to shine the spans of Iranian "Shahmed", as well as a module or system -module when the sounds of outputs are fuzzy. Bazazvis for determining goals is constantly updated, up to calibers less than 82 millimeters. By the way, the latest version of the complex barak is already actively used directly on the Odessa coast.

  • Modules can be controlled remotely?

  • So. If the operator receives from the air intelligence data about the work of the artillery -protector that leads fire on us, and barak it "does not see" at all, Vinidststentally makes a restart of a module, seeks and changes frequency -determination, etc. The operator also has the opportunity to process the obtained data with software algorithms, which, according to the expert, will determine the most precise coordinates of the goals. The data obtained shall be transmitted to the senior boss, who already enforce the expediency or possibility of using the fire in response.

  • As far as I know, there are no world analogues of the world at all. At least by dimensions, survivability, mobility, ease of application and service, width of the observation strip and accuracy during the coverage of a total number of goals. And most importantly - it has a passive effect, it is planned to detect any technical means. He is not capable of influencing the enemy radio struggle. Moreover, it is planted to destroy it physically, such as acoustic intelligence station for a false or armored database. Try to find in the fields and forestry in a few kilometers eight dug and masked under the locality or soils of the case with a suitcase-diploma!Even if the number of them will be accidentally destroyed or failed, the complex will act. The module does not give any radiation, even thermal, and how operators receive information from them - the "secret of the firm".

  • How long does the algorithm take: "Severe" Coordinates goals - data transfer - a decision - a fire in response?

  • Five seconds to determine coordinates, 30 seconds for processing and transferring data to an artillery group, a few minutes to make a decision to impress the target and set the fire task of the artillery unit, and the first shot.

  • The results are satisfactory?

  • More than. In addition to the direct hits, which are constantly in place, we are even naximal shooting distances for errors in determining the coordinates of 50 meters, we can, say, calculations of enemy guns and the guns of the gun-fugitive projectile, fragments of which are flew in a radius of 200 meters. But we or the means of impression of the higher command have a mobile opportunity to suppress the work of the enemy's art to support the action of our possessive.

  • ** Vitaliy Ivanovich, in your opinion, is it capable of barak to take place in the artillery units of our troo

- As far as I understand, barak is simply a short name of the complex, he does not have an industrial manufacturer. But how does the inventor qualify him?

  • The definition of the author sounds as follows: "The centralized multi -moderate system of the reconnaissance of the passive principle." And barak is really an abbreviation.

  • We can see the work of operators barak ?

  • So. A officer from the Fire Support Department of the brigade, who is engaged in this direction, will now be coming behind you. You will see the command of operators, which alternates on the complex and shifting, serves modules, exhibits them according to the schemes and replaces the power supply ...

… We talk to the head of the department, the senior operator of complex -reconnaissance Yaroslav.

- Yaroslav, how much do you think is effective barak ?

  • In terms of accuracy of determining the coordinates of shooting guns or reactive systems of volley fire, it is extremely accurate at distances somewhere in 25 kilometers, and gives a small error at the maximum distance of determining the targets of 30 kilometers. Moreover, we already clearly shine the work not only of mortar calibers, but also anti -aircraft installations and even large caliber machine guns 10-12 thousand meters.

  • Does the quality of work depend on weather conditions or other factors?

  • We have six methods of information processing. Four of them take into account the meteodans, which we enter into the program. Each module gives out the results of the "seam" coordinates autonomously. They are combined in a special plate, after which we receive data on the direction of conducting fire - that is, where the orcs are firing, the distance to their firearms, and in the end - their current coordinates. Then we compare the result with the data of the subdivision, with which we are on online communication, and at night additional with information of the respective points at the leading positions. Then we give out the most exact result where it is necessary.

  • How protected in all senses the modules themselves? - modules give failures?

  • Sometimes. But they are able to restart either independently or remotely with the help of operators. By the way, remote control is a single plus barak. There were several cases where the enemy's work was recorded at any of the directions of the speech, and our complex did not hear it. We remotely reconciled the work of several modules into a different frequency range quickly fell out the enemy. Further, our arta was taken for the cause.

  • You know about the results of her work?

  • I know, but I will not voice. When the older command expresses gratitude to us, it means that we and our artillery worked perfectly.

  • Your impression of barak ?

  • He is incredible!

P . S . ** Sond the interview, the author contacted Odessa, namely, and invented _barak(He has now asked for his name). За його словами, цей комплекс вже ефективно працює не тільки наДонецькому напрямку, але й уздовж узбережжя Чорного моря, в акваторії Очакова,у багатьох бойових бригадах на півдні України. Завдяки БАРАК вони посилиликонтрбатарейну боротьбу з орками та вже навчилися виявляти й знищуватиіранські «Шахеди». Команда однодумців у винахідника велика, наразі вона працюєна волонтерських засадах. Про стовідсоткову готовність комплексу до серійноговиробництва, зі слів винахідника, можна буде говорити лише післядержвипробувань та прийняття його на озброєння в ЗСУ._

EU in the European Union is planned to introduce an "euro"

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-28T-13:11:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T19:11:00+03:00

Description: The European Commission proposes to introduce an electronic euro, while maintaining the circulation of cash and banknotes. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16739...']

Tags: ['Євросоюз', 'Гроші', 'Євро']

Type: Article

The European Commission proposes to introduce an electronic euro, while maintaining cash coins and banknotes.

Such proposals are published on the European Commission's website, Ukrinform reports.

"The European Commission today has released two proposals that have to provide citizens and businesses to make payments by banknotes and coins of Vevrozon, as well as to create framework conditions for a possible introduction of a new digit form of the euro, which the European central bank can create to the intestinal bank," .

It is noted in the euro area and beyond the survey that about 60% of respondents would like to maintain cash use. At the same time, more and more people in the EU make electronic payments accustomed to bank cards or payment applications, which became particularly comprehensive during the Covid-19 pandemic .

Read also: National Bank will control the exchange of currency and banks by exchangersThe first regulatory proposal of the European Commission protects cash Euro-volume, which ensures its payment capacity and accessibility as a payment unit for individuals and businesses in the euro area. In some EU countries, problems have already begun to emerge with restricted people's access to cash due to the reduction of the number of ATMs and bank offices. National governments should be addressed by national governments.

The second regulatory proposal involves providing citizens to EUand European business can make payments using euro electronic currency, a wide circulation, will be a cheap, reliable and stable payment unit for cash. Such a step should strengthen the position of the euro as an international payment unit and strengthen the monetary sovereignty of the EU. The introduction of electronic currency of the euro is also important in view of the development of the cryptocurrency market.

For the convenience of using a digital euro, it is proposed to provide the ability to pay "from the device to the device", even with the absence of pre -ternet access, with the proper level of reliability of payments and protection of personal data.

It was reported that the European Union pursues a purposeful policy to support reforms and strengthen financial stability in EU countries, in particular the spread of the circulation of a single European currency. To date, 20 countries are in Eurogroups: Austria, Belgium, Cyprus, Estonia, Finland, France, Germany, Greece, Ireland, Italy, Spain, Latvia, Lithuania, Luxembourg, Malta, Netherlands, Portugal, Slovakia, Slovenia and Slovenia.

According to the results of a survey conducted by UkrAgroconsult with the Ukrainian grain Association, most Ukrainian farmers expect high wheat yield in 2023, including 64% of the interviewee that it will exceed 5 tons per hectare.

According to Ukrinform, it reports press service of UZA."Expected yield indicators are quite high and make up from 3 to 8t/ha. Make farms(64%)It expects that the yield will exceed 5t/ha. The most optimistic farms of the west and the south of the country, the worst -wave - in the north. The weighted average yield is 5.46t/ha, "the message reads.

It is noted that larger by the wheat areas of the farm will receive higherness due to better technologies. Polls show that farms with wheat above 500 ha are most effective. The lowest yield is expected to farms less than 100 hectares.

In doing so, the vast majority of farms(58%)It expects that the year of wheat will be no worse than the past. Including 12% of the respondent is a yield of yield, especially in the central region.

At the same time, 42%are expected in the north, mainly in the north. It is the intake part that is a significant proportion of farms that have been composed of moisture, reduction of fertilizer application and use of PPPs.

The excess moisture was observed in single cases in the west and north.Despite the difficult material status of the farms, and significant reduction of production during the previous season, almost half of the farms(48%)She was able to make fertilizers at the level not lower than last year. Including 5%of farms even increased introduction, especially in the south of the country.

At the same time, farms that reduced the use of fertilizers, one of the causes the lack of moisture in the soil in the required period. Polls showed the use of liquid fertilizers.

The UZA notes that based on the operational data of the Ministry of Agrarian Policy on sowy and spring, and using the received yields of yields in Ukraine in Ukraine, the gross harvest of wheat in 2023 can be 24.4 million TV raw weights or 23.5 - 24 million tonnes in weight after Refines. This is significantly exceeding the current market expectations, which according to UZA are 15.6 - 18 million.

Category: News

The large -scale invasion of the Russian army into Ukraine has once again renovated that today a reliable protection of the country requires an exceptional efficiency system of air defense. Events in Ukraine are forced to improve the integrated system of reference and missile defense of NATO on the North Atlantic Alliance(IAMD).

Breaking Defense коротко описує загальні принципи роботи системи. Отже,загрози з повітря спочатку виявляють за допомогою датчиків, які здатнівиявляти пуски ракет чи зліт літаків через лічені хвилини після того, як цевідбулося, — спостереження ведеться як з землі, так і з моря, повітря танавіть за допомогою космічних супутників. Усі дані передаються на командніпункти НАТО, як-от Об’єднані центри повітряних операцій (Caoc)in Wedem(Germany)and Torrehoni(Spain). Потім відповідні структури можутьвизначити найкращий спосіб боротьби із загрозою.

Tasks can perform high-ranging missile defense systems, such as US defense system at high altitude(THAAD)or French missiles Sol-Air Moyenne Portée/Terrestre(SAMP/T)small and average. NATO can also use anti -rocket deficiency warships or fighters to effectively counteract threats.

Breaking Defense emphasizes that in recent years, the Alliance has had to deal with new threats, such as unmanned devices and hypersonic rockets. Therefore, NATO is now working hard on tactics and technologies for counteracting these. For example, in the year, Germany proposed a new initiative to the creation of a joint missile and prototypical defense system, called the "European Sky Shield", NATO. And as they set out in Berlin and Brussels, this security program is primarily aimed at increasing the security of NATO countries from air threats and provides even more close and effective integration of air and missing systems of allies into a single complex.

_ Prepared Valery Gastynshchikov_

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T15:55:55+03:00

Images: ['630_360_16879...']

Tags: ['Космос', 'Астрономія', 'Телескоп']

Type: Article

The telescope of the European Southern Observatory recently took pictures, and on June 27, it published an image of nebula, which in the form is very reminiscent of the ore of cat.

As Ukrinform reports, it reports Inverse.

This nebula, known as SH2-284, is an area of dense gas and dust, deforming new stars.

One particularly striking accumulation of newborn stars, called Dolidze 25, burns in the heart of the brightest nebulae area(Under the cat's nose.). Ці молоді масивні зорі наповнюють навколишній простір потужнимизоряними вітрами та інтенсивним випромінюванням, накопичуючи електрони знавколишніх хмар водню.

This ionized hydrogen gas glows with a bright orange and red colorful image in the telescope. That is why SH2-84 is similar to a red cat.

Read also: Hubble showed a bright cluster in the constellation of SagittariusStar winds from Dolidze 25 also repel gas from clusters, forming a vegetation in the center of nebula and collecting gas moving in the wind, into tights, which can eventually generate new stars.

If you look closely at the star cluster, you can see pillars of more thickening gas and dust, which are strong enough so as not to be blurred with starry lights. These pillars give rise to their own clusters of bright stars.

As reported by Ukrinform, space telescope NASA/Esa Hubble photographed a bright spherical cluster of NGC 6544, located in the constellation of Sagittarius.

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T16:14:00+03:00

Description: Today, on June 28, a sculpture of the giant "Mr. Arbitrium" was installed in Lviv near the Opera House. The statue of 5.5 meters of authorship of the Italian sculptor Emanuel Jiannelli illustrates the support of Ukraine during the war. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16879...']

Tags: ['Італія', 'Культура', 'Львів', 'Опера', 'Скульптура']

Type: Article

Today, on June 28, a sculpture of the giant "Mrsterbeitrium" was installed in Lviv near the Opera House. The statue of 5.5 meters of authorship of the Italian sculptorimanel Jiannelli illustrates the support of Ukraine during the war.

According to Ukrinform, it reports the site of the Lviv City Council.This project is the plan of the artist of the fountain, embodied by the sculptor of Emanuhageziannelli. The idea of an Italian artist, Mr. Arbitrium is a figure of a man who "pushes and holds." It was for this peculiarity that he was chosen to Ukraine's message of hope, to support the people and the state at this time the sorrow of the tap, and to repel the war, giving the space of peace and rebuilding.

"I am very glad that Mr. Arbitrium was installed next to the Lviv opera. Men are pleased to realize that this sculptureIt will support Ukrainian art, history and culture. In addition, I want my project to become real support for all artists, musicians, actors and cultural and art figures of Ukraine - I think of quiet Ukrainian artists who have died, suffer, or cannot work with super -cultural projects, giving the beauty of thought to their country and all the world . I express my hope for the accession of Ukraine to the pre -European community as soon as possible and I want to be heard not from an artist from Italy, but an artist of Europe, ”said the author of sculpture Emanuel Jiannelli.

The curator of the project, the artist of the corner of the fountain has been working with Ukrainian institutions for 20 years. She says it is important for her to support Ukrainians today with the help of art.

“Almost eight months ago, I thought about a cultural project that could have performed an important message to my dear Ukraine, so I immediately came to the mind of Mr. Arbitrium - a symbol of strength and stability. We want the Mrstearbitrium to become a great messenger of peace, and we hope that his presence will be a pleasure for all, ”said the corner of the fountain.

The mayor of Lviv emphasized that the sculpture appeared in Lviv precisely the provision of the Constitution as a symbol of support for the Ukrainian people.

He emphasized that there will be discussions around this sculpture, but art has a dialogue for this in order to encourage us to think.

The sculpture of the giant near the Lviv Opera was installed as part of the Lviv Urban Forum. Hundreds of architects and urbanists will come to the city for three days.

Type: Article

The Verkhovna Rada of Ukraine has already submitted a bill, which strengthens the responsibility of labor crimes in the field of justice.

This was reported by the People's Deputy of Ukraine, Chairman of the Verkhovna Rada Committee on Law Policy Denis Maslov on the air of the Tele scale "Unified News", Ukrinform reports.

"Today, a bill that has indeed enhances criminal liability for corruption crimes in the sphere of justice has already been filed for registration in the Verkhovna Rada," he informed.

Read also: [NSDC proposes to strengthen the liability(https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-society/3728859-rnbo-proponue-posiliti-vidpovidalnist-suddiv-za-korupciu-prezident.html)

The People's Deputy stressed that the bill applies not only to judges of the apparatus of judges, “it applies to everyone who gives bribes, who provokes them, and those who promise to resolve the case requires bribes. That is, it is to be aware of everyone without exception. "

"Corruption involved will no longer be able to go on other, lighter articles," Maslov emphasized.

At the same time, he noted that one of the qualifying features, which will enhance the responsibility, will be the commission corruption Crime in martial law.

“In addition, as President Zelensky has announced, the subjects of legislative initiative will be considered, the possibility of applying the polygraph to a candidate's position of judges, as well as to the existing judges in various procedures. We must approach the issue of integrity quite seriously, ”the Parliamentary Committee of the Verkhovna Rada emphasized.

Read also: [the government removed corruption risks in the sale(https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-economy/3728582-urad-pribrav-korupcijni-riziki-pri-prodazu-cinnostej-derzrezervu-minekonomiki.html)

Maslov explained that the polygraph is only one of the tools that can add transparency to the judicial system.

According to the People's Deputy, this instrument will force the whole judge of the corps and those who are undergoing a competition for the position of judge, "think about what will have to pass the polygraph", and this will restrain them from corruption.

"In addition, it will be a source of information to make decisions when specific complaints about judges' actions will be considered, or other issues of their responsibility are resolved," he summarized.As reported by Ukrinform, on June 28, President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky informed during his speech in the Verkhovna Rada of Ukraine about the proposal of the NSDC on the reinforcement of liability of judges and judicial employees for the crimes of the Urrh of Justice and Corruption.

South Korea citizens from now on "younger" for at least a year

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-28T16:56:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T23:56:00+03:00

Description: In South Korea, a law that coordinates the methods of calculating age with international standards came into force. After that, all the citizens of the LCD were "younger" for a year or two. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_14780...']

Tags: ['Корея', 'Закон']

Type: Article

Condition of Korea came into force by a law that coordinates the methods of calculating the age -old standards. After that, all the citizens of the LCD were "younger" for a year or two.

About it reports BBC, reports Ukrinform.

The law adopted last year in December abolishes the South Korean tradition, which is a year at birth year(Given pre -natal development)And from January 1, it gets older a year. That is, the child, which was angered on December 31, was two years next day.

The system at which the age is calculated by subtracting the year of birth from the current one without consideration of months is also abolished.

Thus, as of June 28, 2023, a person born on June 29, 2003, was 19 years old on an international system, 20 years under the age of "calculating age" and 21 years under the system " Korean Age ».

Now the system of calculating age in Korea is unified.

Read also: South Korea this year will hold the first for the 10 -year parade

The incumbent President of Korea Yun Jok Yol strongly insisted on the necessary changes during the election campaign. According to him, traditional methods of age calculations have led to "unnecessary social and economic expenditures". For example, there were disputes over insurance payments and determination of the right to participate in state assistance programs.

Japan adopted the International Standard for Calculating Age in 1950, and Northern Korea followed this example in the 1980s.

News Source: https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-world/3728977-gromadani-pivdennoi-korei-vidsogodni-pomolodsali-sonajmense-na-rik.html

“In order to limit the opportunities of Russia and Belarus to continue fighting in Ukraine that pose a threat to Lithuania's safety, LithuaniaIt is taking decisive action - we will limit the export of double -purpose goods to third countries through Russia and Belarus, ” - commented on the decision of the Ministry of Economy and Innovation Auschrina Armoite.

The proposal to replenish the list of prohibited dual -use goods was made by the Ministry of Economy and Innovation. The Lithuanian government assumed it. The decision comes into force on July 3, 2023 and will operate on January 2 until 201024.

According to the resolution, Lithuanian Economics undertakes to inform the European Commission and the ESPRO member states established export prohibition.

Lithuanian media specifythat the list is replenished for 57 groups of dual -use goods, these are predominantly documents with microelectronic and semiconductor components. "Some details are installed in washing machines, and some in weapons," Armone said.

The Minister of Economy stressed that a new order is not a sanction, but only restraint. “We have informed the European Commission. The most effective would be(Common - ed.)The European decision is that such goods do not pass through Latvia, Finland Tanorwegia, ”Armoite said.Foreign Minister Gabrielus Landsbergis added that after making such a decision at the national level Lithuania, there is a risk that land paths through other neighboring countries will be used to bypass. The National Commission commented on the decision to rename Zaporozhye

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-28T18:14:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T18:14:00+03:00

Description: The National State Language Commission emphasizes the recommendation nature of the proposals for the renaming of Zaporozhye. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16879...']

Tags: ['Українська мова', 'Перейменування', 'Запоріжжя']

Type: Article

The National Language Commission on the National Language Standards emphasize the nominative nature of the proposal for the renaming of Zaporozhye.

This was reported by the Chairman of the National Commission Volodymyr Mozgunov during the preparation in Ukrinform.

"Рішення комісії - це висловлені рекомендації, рішення комісії - це неперейменування населених пунктів, у нас немає на це повноважень. У будь-якомуразі це має вирішувати громада, органи місцевого самоврядування", - сказаввін.

Мозгунов зауважив, що рішення комісії мають рекомендаційний характер, щобзвернути увагу органів місцевого самоврядування на проблеми.

У свою чергу, член Нацкомісії зі стандартів державної мови Ольга Новіковазаявила, що на сьогодні в наукових колах є різні тлумачення таких назв, як " Запоріжжя "and" Zaporozhye ".

"The position of the commission lies in the fact that both that and that name we consider it correct, they meet the standards of Ukrainian literary language," she explained.

In addition, she said that the National Commission was addressed from the residents of the resident to consider the renaming of the city, after which the commission reconciled with this issue to the working group, which was taken care of by the issues of permeation.

Images: ['630_360_16879...']

Tags: ['Львівщина', 'Міст', 'Ремонт', 'Відбудова']

Type: Article

The State Agency for Recovery and Development of Infrastructure opened the movement of the bridge on the Roziliv - Radekhiv - Lutsk near the village of Gayok, in the Lviv region.

About it reports Ukrinform with reference to the press service Agencishable. “We improve the connection between Lviv and Lutsk. The movement was opened by 140 meters on the road in Lviv - Radekhiv - Lutsk near the village of Gayok. From 2:00 pm, the tidyanka of the highway is opened for passage of cars and public transport. The trucks will need to use the detour for some time, according to the previously approved scheme, ”the message reads.

The agency said that during 2021 and 2023 roads dismantled the construction of the old bridge, arranged piles and piles of supports, mounted 36 beams of the run structure, installed deformation seams, and also staged a reinforced concrete monolithic plate and transitional slabs, waterproofing and drainage, two Sharosfalt concrete coating.

Read also: [in Mykolaiv region another bridge through the Riverwolf] was rebuilt](https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-vidbudova/3728516-na-mikolaivsini-vidbuduvali-se-odin-mist-cerez-ricku-ingulec.html)For a full opening of the traffic, in particular, for freight transport it is necessary to equip the top layer of asphalt concrete, barrier enclosure, lighting, apply road marking and install signs. The length of the new bridge will be 141.5 m, the width of the roadway is 9.5 m, sidewalks - 1.8.

The bridge near the village of Gayok on the H-17 highway has been built in 1960-since then Vinzhnaya has not been overhauled. On May 3, 2021, a collapse of the emergency bridge occurred due to the wear of the constructions. In 2022 it was planned to open.

It was reported in Ukraine will create a commission to check the state of bridges, which will be headed by the Viceremier-Minister for Recovery-Oleksandr Kubrakov, Minister of Development of Communities, Territories and Infrastructure.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-28T20:26:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T20:26:00+03:00

Description: The occupation and risk of Russia's terrorist attack at the Zaporozhye Nuclear Power Plant threatens the entire OSCE space. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16833...']

Tags: ['Дмитро Кулеба', 'ОБСЄ', 'Теракт', 'Запорізька АЕС', 'Війна з Росією']

Type: Article

Occupation and the risk of committing a terrorist attack at the Zaporizhzhya Nuclear Power Plant poses the entire space of the OSCE.

This was stated by the Minister of Foreign Affairs of Ukraine Dmytro Kuleba, on the OSCE Presidential Conference on Security Issues, reports Ukrinform with a reference to Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

“Today, Russia is threatening Ukraine and the entire OSCE space of the Radiation Ministry at the Zaporizhzhya Nuclear Power Plant. Whatever the Russian propaganda, Russia, and only Russia has today has motivation and means for it to commit an incident to the ZPP, ”the minister said.

He stressed that, having occupied the station and turning it into a military base, Russia uses the NPP as a nuclear blackmail tool.

"I do not know what else to happen for the OSCE States Parties to recognize the obvious: Russia is not a place at this table," the head of Ukrainian diplomacy emphasized.

This terrorist act has brought the Russian crimes to a new stage, as a real scale of its consequences for people and the environment can only be estimated later.

The Minister expressed gratitude to the chairman of Northern Macedonia for the firm position of protecting the principles of the OSCE in the conditions of full -scale aggression of Russia anti -Ukraine.

“Russia's impunity cannot be tolerated, the illegal detention of employees OSCE, theft is more than 70 vehicles. There can be no discussion with a country whose president is in search of the ISS for the military crime of abduction of Ukrainian children. There can be no civilized dialogue with a country that causes intense blowers and drones in densely populated residential areas, resorts to massives, torture, rape and intimidation of civilians. There can be no understanding of an understanding with an aggressor who is trying to destroy Ukrainian and national identity, ”Kuleba emphasized.*!(https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-society/3728893-v-ukraini-projdut-navcanna-z-podolanna-naslidkiv-mozlivoi-avarii-na-zaes.html)The Ministry of Foreign Affairs of Ukraine called on the OSCE to actively participate in the embodiment of the formula of peace.

“We live in the time of challenges when discussions without pragmatic decisions are no longer working. If we want to preserve the OSCE and our collective devotion to the principles of the Helsinki final act, we need to find a way to suspend Russia in the OSCE, ”the minister summed up.

As it was reported, on March 4, 2022 the Russians occupied the ZPP. June 22, 2023 President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky declaredAbout Russia plans to arrange a terract at the Zaporozhye NPP.

Tags: ['Арешт', 'Хабар', 'Суд', 'Тернопільщина']

Type: Article

The High Anti -Corruption Court elected the chairman of the Ternopil Regional Council, Mikhail, the Headquarters West in the form of detention with the possibility of making 805 thousand UAH of pledge.

The relevant decisions were made by the investigating judge Oleg Tkachenko, informs “Central Protity of Corruption”.

As it is noted, prosecutors of the specialized anti -corruption prosecutor's office were in court about the election of a precautionary measure in the form of detention under guard with the possibility of making 13 million UAH of collateral.

If the amount of Golovko is introduced, it will be necessary to refrain from communicating, withdrawal passports and wearing an electronic bracelet.

South Korea citizens from now on "younger" for at least a year

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-28T23:56:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T23:56:00+03:00

Description: In South Korea, a law that coordinates the methods of calculating age with international standards came into force. After that, all the citizens of the LCD were "younger" for a year or two. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_14780...']

Tags: ['Корея', 'Закон']

Type: Article

Condition of Korea came into force by a law that coordinates the methods of calculating the age -old standards. After that, all the citizens of the LCD were "younger" for a year or two.

About it reports BBC, reports Ukrinform.

The law adopted last year in December abolishes the South Korean tradition, which is a year at birth year(Given pre -natal development)And from January 1, it gets older a year. That is, the child, which was angered on December 31, was two years next day.

The system at which the age is calculated by subtracting the year of birth from the current one without consideration of months is also abolished.

Thus, as of June 28, 2023, a person born on June 29, 2003, was 19 years old on an international system, 20 years under the age of "calculating age" and 21 years under the system " Korean Age ».

Now the system of calculating age in Korea is unified.

Read also: South Korea this year will hold the first for the 10 -year parade

The incumbent President of Korea Yun Jok Yol strongly insisted on the necessary changes during the election campaign. According to him, traditional methods of age calculations have led to "unnecessary social and economic expenditures". For example, there were disputes over insurance payments and determination of the right to participate in state assistance programs.

Japan adopted the International Standard for Calculating Age in 1950, and Northern Korea followed this example in the 1980s.

If a call has received a call from the phone, SMS has been reported to social networks, you should contact the investigator who will investigate the criminal proceedings. He needs to file a petition for the location of the radio electronic agent.

About it informsOleg Kotenko, a commissioner of quitting persons missing in special circumstances.

If the petition is granted, then native persons need:

How to protect yourself in the case of increased radiation level

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-06-28T4:00:00-04:00

Description: DECILE STRACH SORD AREDAY, JAK TRAINED VID Radіetsiyoy Vuvlivvoy. Yakshcho Voidomalen about ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest News Today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia, and when, the war with Ukraine in 2022 will be or not, will there be war With Ukraine, in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['radiacziya.jpg', 'content_dixi_8_03-01.png']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ІНФОГРАФІКА', 'МІНРЕІНТЕГРАЦІЇ']

Category: News

A few simple tips on how to protect from radiation.

If the radioactive contamination message caught you on the street:

  • Go immediately to the nearest room. It is best to choose a shelter or basement. To protect the breathing, cover your nose and mouth with a towel, a handkerchief or put on a medical mask.

If the radioactive contamination message caught you at home:

  • Close all windows, doors and close the ventilation openings. Do not approach them without urgent need and do not go outside. Turn off the air conditioner and heaters. Wear a mask or cotton gauze to protect the respiratory system.

Importantly!Be sure to monitor the rescuers of the SES, police and local authorities. Follow their targeting instructions unconditionally.

Source: Menrointegration

The document proposes to identify the categories of positions whose candidates are obliged to develop English. Requirements for compulsory English are set for persons claiming positions:

Author: ['Анастасія Олехнович']

Tags: ['ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ГЕРОЇ НЕСКОРЕНОЇ УКРАЇНИ!', 'ГЕРОЙ УКРАЇНИ', 'ППО ЗСУ']

Category: News

Today, on June 28, on the Day of the Constitution of Ukraine, President Vladimirzelensky awarded the title of Hero of Ukraine to the colonel Sergiuyaremenko, commander of the 96th Anti-aircraft missile brigade of the Center Air Command.

Since the beginning of a large -scale invasion, Sergei Yaremenko heads a team that kicks off air attacks on the central and northern regions of Ukraine. And most importantly - provides air protection of the capital of our country.

It was the anti-aircraft command under the command of Sergiy Yaremenko on the call sign "Granite" withstood the crazy air attacks on Kiev in May-June, not allowing any more than 200 goals to accurately hit objects, and destroyed 13 "invincible" aerobalist missiles X-47 "dagger". Today, June 28, the Verkhovna Rada of Ukraine adopted the project # 9342dated 29.05.2023 “The Law on Amendments to Certain Legislative Acts of Ukraine on Separate Requests related to the passage of military service during the military station”, according to which the annual leave is increased for servicemen. Also, monthly additional remuneration is provided for servicemen time of combat(special)tasks.

About it reportsThe press service of the Verkhovna Rada of Ukraine.

“Changes are suggested to allow servicemen to use part of the annual leave duration 30 -calendar days with the possibility of division into parts in the course of action.(To date - 10 Calendar Days)», - the message reads.

In addition, during the martial law, military personnel are paid monthly remuneration from 30 to 100 thousand hryvnias proportional to combat execution(special)tasks in order, size and on the conditions established by the Cabinet of Ministers of Ukraine.

Urgent military service is paid on a monthly basis for a monthly reward of 6 thousand hryvnias in proportion to the time of military service.

Servicemen who were injured(injury, injury, injury)related to the protection of the Motherland during the fighting and which are being identified at the disposal of the relevant commander during the temporary container of military service, established by the Military Medical Commission, an additional remuneration of the 6 thousand UAH is paid on a monthly basis.

Cadets of higher military educational institutions, as well as higher educational establishments, which have military institutes in their composition, faculties of military preparation, departments of military preparation are paid on a monthly basis additional Babinorod in the amount 2 350 UAH in proportion to the training time.

Separately, Volodymyr Zelenskyy invited to discuss the provisions of the provisions of the Ukrainian soldiers: from soldiers, sailors and sergeantivo generals.

“No one has the right to determine the fate of Ukraine without asking them, our heroes. And I am everyone and everyone in the defense and security forces of Ukraine - as far as the conditions of war allow - to participate in our general national discussion on the Ukrainian doctrine, ”the heads said.

As a guarantor of the Constitution of Ukraine, the President proposed to the beginning of the general discussion about the Ukrainian doctrine five the main abractions.

The first is the philosophy of our victory.

The second is the globality of Ukrainian security.

The third is the heroes policy.

The fourth is justice policy.

Fifth - Transformation for 10 years(New foreign policy, economy, relations between the state and society, development of territories, education and science, culture, level of security and freedom in Ukraine).

«Це – напрями, які можуть бути розкриті тими чи іншими конкретними пунктами,які нація визначить як важливі», – заначив Президент.

«Свобода – це дитя небайдужості, а безпека – побратим сміливості. Українаперемоги буде країною, достойною своїх героїв», – наголосив Глава держави.

The Secretary General of the United Nations in his report on children of armed conflict for 2023 considers Russia and its settings responsible for the murder of Ukrainian children, as well as for attacks at hospital and school. About it reportsOffice of the Prosecutor General of Ukraine.

The inclusion of the Secretary General of Russia-P5 member in the annual "List of Shame" as parties of the armed conflict responsible for serious violations of children is an important notice to the aggressor state and criminals involved in the committing atrocities in relation to children: such actions are not permitted and are not worried.

We urge the United Nations to closely monitor Russia's actions, and as well as the measures that it pledged to take to improve the protection of Ukrainian children under its effective control.

There is currently no such progress: according to our latest estimates, in the beginning of full -scale aggression of Russia against Ukraine, 493 children were killed and 1033 were injured, almost 20,000 children have been forcibly deported. These are only those cases that are listed in criminal proceedings. These figures do not include temporarily occupied territories, so real figures can be significantly high. In total, in Ukraine, law enforcement agencies are investigating more than 3,000 rays against children.

The international community should be remembered that the desire for peace can not be identified by the victim and the aggressor, since the act of aggression of Russia has led to an armed conflict and continuous commission of cruel crimes in Ukraine by its forces and settings.The Office of the Prosecutor General is working closely with the UN International International Investigation Commission on Ukraine, providing information on the forced movement of Ukrainian children and other serious violations of children's rights from September 2022. Two meetings have been carried out and one request for information was provided. crimes committed against children in the course of Russian aggression.

In Ukraine, a working group was created at the state level on interaction of the special representative of the UN Secretary General for Children and Armed Conflicts. In the course of its work, the Office of the Prosecutor General provides information on severe violations of children by Russia.

Our prosecutors are in contact with experts of the International Criminal Court. More than 40 volumes of cases of cases have been transferred to the Ministry of Internal Affairs, more than 30 requests for the protection of evidence, information and investigative actions have been fulfilled.

We also cooperate with the experts of the Moscow OSCE mechanism. The latest report of the Soming mechanism was dedicated to the protection of the rights of deported Ukrainian children. During its training, the OSCE experts held meetings with prosecutors who carry out procedural guidance in criminal proceedings on the deportation of children and other international crimes committed against children.

Category: News

In accordance with the decision of the National Security and Defense Council of June 23, 2023, the government created a commission to check the state of bridges in Ukraine. Oleksandr Kubrakov, the Minister of Community Development, Territories and Infrastructure.

The task of the commission is to check the transport and operational state of roads on public roads and railway bridges.

“Supporting bridges in a proper condition is, first and foremost, the issue of basic safety people they move. During the martial law, the bridge became an important defense capability of the country, as well as ways for humanitarian evacuation and export logistics. Our task now is to find out the real technical condition of the construction. After that, in conjunction with balancing holders(city and regional administrations)Identify ways to solve problems. I believe that safety and defense should be a top priority for the authorities of any level, ”Alexander Kubrakov reported.

The commission will include representatives of the Ministry of Recovery, the Ministry of Defense, the Ministry of Internal Affairs, the Ministry of Reintegration of the Occupied Territories, the Agency of Restoration, Ukrtrans Security, the State Inspectorate of Architecture and Urban Planning, the State Service of Ukraine of Official Situations, Regional and Kyiv City Military Administrations.

_ What will the commission work? _

To determine the technical condition of the bridges is planned:

· Analysis of primary technical and operational documentation;

· Conducting inspection and inspection of structures;

· Finding the real strength of the materials of the bridge elements;

· Performing checks of load capacity;

· Establishment of real characteristics of elements of elements.

The results of the inspection of the bridges will be entered in a single information analytical and expert system of Aesum to form further steps to restore them.

As of 2023, there are about 28.5 thousand road bridges in Ukraine.

According to the profile research institute "State Dorndi"-the average vicious car bridges-more than 60 years, more than 30% of bridges in critically. About 350 - destroyed or damaged as a result of hostilities.

President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky held a bilateral meeting with the Republic of Poland Andrzej Duda, who is on a visit in Kiev.

The head of the Ukrainian state noted that the presence of Andrzej Duda in Ukraine in the afternoon of the Constitution is an important signal of support for our country, special before NATO Summit in Vilnius.

Leaders coordinated positions on the eve of NATO Summit in Vilnius. Volodymyrzelensky praised the position of the President of Poland on the political invitation of Ukraine to NATO membership.

The heads of state discussed a number of topical issues of bilateral development separately.

“We have repeatedly found solutions for difficult issues. This will meet the high level of relations and the spirit of the strategic partnership of the intersection of states, ”the President of Ukraine summed up.

The President of Ukraine proposes to develop heroes policy on Ukrainian soldiers

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-06-28T99:00:00-04:00

Description: President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky Proponiti in Maybutniykhiykiy ... War with Ukraine 2022, War with Ukraine Latest News Today, News War with Ukraine 2022 Last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia and when the war with Ukraine will be in 2022 Or not, will there be a war with Ukraine in the near future, they say, the war with Ukraine, Ukraine’s news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['6148f8d165ba010270683175ce0e3ca0_1687952457_extra_large.jpeg', '92f05ffed72bbf7fba6205582cc5b4b8_1687952437_wysiwyg.jpeg']

Tags: []

Category: News

President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky proposes to anticipate in the future Ukrainian doctrine the policy of heroes, which will be aimed at providing the need for participants of hostilities and veterans of war. The Head of State stated this, presenting the orientations of the doctrine at the plenary session of the Verkhovna Rada of the Constitution of Ukraine.

“The Ukrainian state needs new principles of gratitude to all who have struggled for the freedom and independence of Ukraine. The invaluable experience of Ukrainian soldiers is effectively used in the process of guaranteeing the world of real security, ”the President emphasized in a speech in the session hall of Parliament.

Among the components of the heroes of Heroes, Volodymyr Zelenskyy called providing the state in the war for soldiers who want to continue to serve Ukraine and the people after the end of the war.

A platform for the export of Ukrainian defense knowledge, practices and experience gained by our warriors during the fighting should also be developed.

"Ukrainians and Ukrainians will be able to share the successful experience of effective protection against full -scale aggression in peacekeeping missions, in particular under ehydyoon, training international missions, etc., because after victory we will have even such important and valuable experience ... - the head of state is convinced.

Unique combat experience should also be used in new system education in Ukraine, the President said.

“Ukrainian soldiers and all who train Ukrainian soldiers should know that real practitioners will be the basis of new Ukrainian military education. The state integrated the training programs that have now shown their effectiveness, as well as the real -focus of our soldiers and sailors, sergeants, officers, officers, our generics into the military education system, ”he said.

In addition, according to the President, complete integration of veterans into the social and economic life of the country, in particular by acquiring a military related civilian specialty, creating a system of support and their relatives on the principle of "equal with equal".The President also spoke for the introduction of a real national standard for heroes: new requirements for urban planning, infrastructure, public space, transport, social and educational systems, business environment.

“Ukraine has to create the strongest rehabilitation industry in Europe. This applies to the construction of rehabilitation centers and the preparation of appropriate personnel. The state will help to create the required number of jobs, not only to ensure rehabilitation for our people, but also to have the opportunity to have a stitched exporter of renewal and integration practices into the post -war life absolutely for anyone who has passed and He was injured from the war, ”the heads said.

According to Volodymyr Zelensky, Ukraine should introduce the best practices and the most effective politicians for Ukrainians and Ukrainians to endure the pain, stress and injuries of war.

"In particular, we must finally be honestly legalized for anyone who needs it, cannabis -based medicines, relevant research and controlled Ukrainian production," the President added.

Veterans should also be involved in public service in Ukraine, they should be complicated by councils of different levels, including in the Verkhovna Rada.

“To work veterans is an honor for any business. To help me to start their own business is an honor for the state, for every community, for every business association, and for anyone who knows what means to be swallowed. And it should not be a dream, but a reality in Ukraine, ”he said that it should be a large -scale national task.

According to the Head of State, heroes should become an important component of the heroes' policies, in particular the memorialization of war and the experience of Ukraine's victory.

“Creation of the Pantheon of Heroes and the National Military Cemetery. The creation of the National Museum of the Russian-Ukrainian War and the system of local museums that honor the memory of the war and preserve the experience of victory for the subsequent cans of the Ukrainian people, ”Volodymyr Zelenskyy said.

It is also about creative understanding of the experience of war, export of the experience of our victory by means of culture, the creation of the official history of war, the definition of a nationally canon of interpretation of war with Russia - participants of war, its clavial events, stages, Russian crimes of war and the achievements of the Ukrainian respects.Source: Presidential Ukrainian site

The Mariupol Reborn Mariupol Reconstruction Project was launched in Lviv

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-06-28T9:23:43+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-06-28T22:23:43+03:00

Description: In Lviv, the platform of strategic and architectural modeling "Mariuupol Reborn" was opened with the concept of renewal of the future city, which was presented by four teams of urbanists. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16850...']

Tags: ['Маріуполь', 'Війна з Росією', 'Відбудова']

Type: Article

The opening of the Strategic and Architectural Modeling of Mariuupol Reborn was opened in Lviv from the concept of restoring the future city, which presented the Urban team.

This was reported by Ukrinform correspondent.

“Mariupol became the heart of Ukraine. If we restore it, then Yukraine will recover. But this is a great responsibility. Therefore, this platform "Mariupol Reborn" is an opportunity to form a future vision of the reconstruction of the city together, ”said Mariupol Camivsky chairman Vadim Boychenko.

According to Boychenko, "Mariupol Reborn" is a platform that corresponds to the development of an infrastructure restoration plan, the creation of an architectural plan for reconstruction of the city and the creation of an international investment platform.

The project is being implemented by the Mariupol City Council on behalf of Pavlakirilenko, the head of the Donetsk Ova, as well as with the support of the EBRD, the World Bank, the USAID Project "Economic Support of Ukraine" and SCM.

Read also: Russians continue to demolish high -rise buildings in Mariupe OliBoychenko stated that in 15 months, since the full -scale invasion of Russia, Mariupol city authorities built a stable system "I Mariupol" - 21 Center in Ukraine, where Mariupols found support and shelter. But, according to its words, many efforts are also aimed at developing a road card of returning home and reconstruction of the hometown near the sea. It is now known that more than 90% of buildings in the city are affected, another 50% are completely destroyed. Only preliminary estimates, the cost of recovering $ 14.5 billion.

The opening of the platform in Lviv is just the first step. In the further plans of the city IDA Mariupol - the involvement of international expertise. To do this, the space will appear in Warsaw, Poland.

“It is there that we want to get that important expertise that will give us knowledge. Polyshch has the experience of restoring cities after the war. It was a system that is the purpose of Mariupol, ”the mayor added.

The mayor of Lviv Andriy Sadovy stressed that everyone in Ukraine dreams of a pro -performance. But do not forget about the important stage - the reconstruction of cities.

During the presentation of the project, four teams of urbanists presented their concepts of future restoration and restructuring Mariupol.

As reported by Ukrinform, during the blockade, the invaders destroyed 50% of all residential fund of Mariupol. More than 300 homes have completely taken out the post -occupation. At the same time, many Mariupols fight for them to be home to them, because they continue to live there.

Russia's aggression caused one of the largest humanitarian catastrophes in Mariupol. The city was almost 90% destroyed as a result of enemy shelling, and here and the non -normative supply of electricity, water, gas.

In addition, the invaders wear the damaged homes to hide the trace crimes.

The enemy transforms Mariupol and the surrounding settlements into a military-logistics hub.

The military personnel of the Armed Forces of Ukraine study vital skills of life on the battlefield on the first of their kind of combat training, which is conducted by the British army and its international partners.

!(Images/AРМІЯINFORM/2023-06-29T98-00-00-04-00/356647122_613474257632323_7896844699036819464_n-150x150.jpg)

During the five weekly course, which began on May 29, Ukrainian physicians were critically important, such as: providing medical care, monitoring high blood loss and providing emergency care with the high -speed stage.

The organizers note that the program took into account the evidence of the battle and requests of the Ukrainian military. During the training of the students, they also studied how best to optimize their own health in order to be ready to work in combat conditions, and they could test their knowledge in practice close to real combat -combat tesks in order to gain confidence in the efficient use of their skills on the forefront. They include:

  • mass examination of the wounded with various injuries;

  • providing assistance to victims with serious injuries caused by shooting with small arms;

  • ways of safe evacuation of victims of civil and military transport;

  • evacuation of the wounded under fire.

!(Images/AРМІЯINFORM/2023-06-29T98-00-00-04-00/356636163_613474277632321_5277639290003837670_n-150x150.jpg)

In the next few days of study, Ukrainian servicemen of Tavi servicemen will learn to provide first aid to other military servicemen of the Armed Forces of Ukraine after returning to the forefront.

The current course is the first of the three programs of combat medical training, and about 50 Ukrainian servicemen are planned to be prepared during the Quarantee.
